#ammunition
increase_ammunition_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		ammunition_market_panel_quantity <= 1000000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_market_panel_quantity
				var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity < 1000000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_market_panel_quantity
				add = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		ammunition_market_panel_quantity > 50000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_market_panel_quantity
				var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity > 50000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_market_panel_quantity
				subtract = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}

				var:tools_market_panel_quantity > 50000

#ammunition
buy_ammunition_budget_panel = {
	effect = {
		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = international_buy_ammunition_budget_panel
			#add = international_buy_ammunition_budget_panel
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_ammunition_state_1
					add = owner.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					name = stockpiling_aeroplanes_state_1

				}
			}
		}
	}

sell_limit_var_show = {
	is_shown = {
		var:sell_limit_var_1 > 0
	}
}

sell_limit_var_show_0 = {
	is_shown = {
		var:sell_limit_var_1 = 0
	}
}

#ammunition
buy_ammunition_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price
				value = ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = ammunition_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_ammunition_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_1
				value  = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price
				value = scope:target.ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.ammunition_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_ammunition_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_ammunition_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_ammunition_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.ammunition_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_ammunition_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#ammunition quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_1
				value  = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#ammunition price
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price
				value = ammunition_price
			}

			#ammunition price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = ammunition_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = ammunition_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_ammunition_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_ammunition_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_ammunition_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_ammunition_var_state > player.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_ammunition_market_panel
		player.var:ammunition_contract_1_year = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_ammunition_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_ammunition_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_ammunition_var_state > player.var:ammunition_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_ammunition_market_panel
		player.var:ammunition_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_ammunition_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################
#small_arms
buy_small_arms_market_panel = {
	effect = {

				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#small_arms quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#small_arms price
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_sell_price
				value = small_arms_price
			}

			#small_arms price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = small_arms_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_small_arms_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#small_arms quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_buy_1
				value  = var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#small_arms price
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_buy_price
				value = scope:target.small_arms_price
			}

			#small_arms price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.small_arms_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_small_arms_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_small_arms_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

buy_small_arms_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_small_arms_var_state > player.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_small_arms_market_panel
		player.var:small_arms_contract_1_year = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_small_arms_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_small_arms_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_small_arms_var_state > player.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_small_arms_market_panel
		player.var:small_arms_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:small_arms_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}

			text = sell_small_arms_custom_tooltip
		}
	}

		}

			}

					multiply = artillery_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {

			# 	value = 1

buy_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:grain_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
####################################################################################################################################################

#####################################################################################################################################################
#fabric
buy_fabric_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#fabric quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#fabric price
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_price
				value = fabric_price
			}

			#fabric price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = fabric_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_fabric_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#fabric quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_1
				value  = var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#fabric price
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_price
				value = scope:target.fabric_price
			}

			#fabric price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.fabric_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_fabric_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_fabric_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_fabric_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#fabric quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#fabric price
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.fabric_price
			}

			#fabric price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.fabric_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_fabric_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#fabric quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_1
				value  = var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#fabric price
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_price
				value = fabric_price
			}

			#fabric price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = fabric_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = fabric_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_fabric_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_fabric_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_fabric_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_fabric_var_state > player.var:fabric_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_fabric_market_panel
		player.var:fabric_contract_1_year = 0
		var:fabric_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_fabric_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		# not  = {

		player.var:fabric_contract_1_year = 0

				name = order_buy_paper_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_paper_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#paper quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:paper_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#paper price
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.paper_price
			}

			#paper price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:paper_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.paper_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_paper_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#paper quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_sell_1
				value  = var:paper_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#paper price
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_sell_price
				value = paper_price
			}

			#paper price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = paper_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:paper_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = paper_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = paper_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_paper_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_paper_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_paper_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_paper_var_state > player.var:paper_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_paper_market_panel
		player.var:paper_contract_1_year = 0
		var:paper_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_paper_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_paper_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah

		player.stockpiling_paper_var_state > player.var:paper_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_paper_market_panel
		player.var:paper_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:paper_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}

		}

		}
	}

####################################################################################################################################################

#####################################################################################################################################################
#iron
buy_iron_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#iron quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#iron price
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_price
				value = iron_price
			}

			#iron price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = iron_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_iron_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#iron quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_1
				value  = var:iron_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#iron price
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_price
				value = scope:target.iron_price
			}

			#iron price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:iron_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.iron_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = iron_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_iron_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_iron_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_iron_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

			#iron quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#iron price
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.iron_price
			}

			#iron price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.iron_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_iron_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#iron quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_1
				value  = var:iron_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#iron price
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_price
				value = iron_price
			}

			#iron price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = iron_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:iron_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = iron_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = iron_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_iron_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_iron_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_iron_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_iron_var_state > player.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_iron_market_panel
		player.var:iron_contract_1_year = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_iron_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_iron_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_iron_var_state > player.var:iron_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_iron_market_panel
		player.var:iron_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:iron_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_iron_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				name = oil_sell_1
				value  = var:oil_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#oil price
			set_variable = {
				name = oil_sell_price
				value = oil_price
			}

			#oil price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = oil_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:oil_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = oil_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = oil_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_oil_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_oil_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_oil_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_oil_var_state > player.var:oil_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_oil_market_panel
		player.var:oil_contract_1_year = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_oil_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_oil_market_panel_enabled = {

		# not  = {

		player.var:oil_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:oil_release_status = 0

			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply

#engines
buy_engines_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#engines quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:engines_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#engines price
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_sell_price
				value = engines_price
			}

			#engines price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:engines_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = engines_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_engines_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#engines quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_buy_1
				value  = var:engines_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#engines price
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_buy_price
				value = scope:target.engines_price
			}

			#engines price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = engines_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:engines_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.engines_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = engines_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_engines_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_engines_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

			}

			# 	name = sell_explosives_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#explosives quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = explosives_buy_1
				value  = var:explosives_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#explosives price
			set_variable = {
				name = explosives_buy_price
				value = scope:target.explosives_price
			}

			#explosives price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = explosives_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:explosives_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.explosives_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = explosives_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_explosives_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_explosives_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

				value = 1

				value = 1

				name = order_sell_explosives_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_explosives_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_explosives_var_state > player.var:explosives_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_explosives_market_panel
		player.var:explosives_contract_1_year = 0
		var:explosives_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_explosives_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_explosives_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_explosives_var_state > player.var:explosives_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_explosives_market_panel
		player.var:explosives_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:explosives_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_explosives_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				value = 1

			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_opium_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_opium_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_opium_var_state > player.var:opium_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_opium_market_panel
		player.var:opium_contract_1_year = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_opium_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_opium_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_opium_var_state > player.var:opium_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_opium_market_panel
		player.var:opium_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0
		player.var:opium_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = {
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_opium_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				name = trade_dinar_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

		effect = {
			set_variable = {
				name = trade_dinar_var
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}

#ammunition
#quatituy
increase_ammunition_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
		#var:ammunition_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
				#var:ammunition_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
		var:ammunition_store_quantity > 1000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
				var:ammunition_store_quantity > 1000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_ammunition_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
		ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
				ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
		var:ammunition_release_quantity > 1000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
				var:ammunition_release_quantity > 1000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
#time
increase_ammunition_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_month
		var:ammunition_store_month < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_month
		var:ammunition_store_month > 12
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_store_month
				var:ammunition_store_month > 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_ammunition_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_month
		ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_month
		var:ammunition_release_month > 12
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_release_month
				var:ammunition_release_month > 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

set_ammunition_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_ammunition
				remove_modifier = releasing_ammunition
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_ammunition_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_ammunition_var_1 < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		var:ammunition_store_quantity > 0 
	}
} 
set_store_ammunition = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_ammunition_var_1
			value = ammunition_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_month_fixe
			value = var:ammunition_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_ammunition
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_ammunition
					multiplier = ammunition_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_ammunition_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_ammunition_var_1
			value = ammunition_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_ammunition
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_ammunition
					multiplier = ammunition_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes

	}

set_release_ammunition_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state

		ammunition_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_ammunition = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_var_1
			value = ammunition_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_month_fixe
			value = var:ammunition_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity_1_year
			value = ammunition_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_ammunition
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_ammunition
					multiplier = ammunition_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_small_arms_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
		#var:small_arms_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
				#var:small_arms_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:small_arms_store_status = 0
				var:small_arms_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = small_arms_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_small_arms_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
		var:small_arms_store_quantity > 1000
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = small_arms_store_quantity
				var:small_arms_store_quantity > 1000
				var:small_arms_store_status = 0
				var:small_arms_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = small_arms_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_small_arms_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = small_arms_release_quantity
		small_arms_release_predicted < stockpiling_small_arms_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = small_arms_release_quantity
				small_arms_release_predicted < stockpiling_small_arms_var_state
				var:small_arms_store_status = 0
				var:small_arms_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = small_arms_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_small_arms_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = small_arms_release_quantity
		var:small_arms_release_quantity > 1000
		var:small_arms_store_status = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = small_arms_release_quantity
				var:small_arms_release_quantity > 1000
				var:small_arms_store_status = 0
				var:small_arms_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = small_arms_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_small_arms
				remove_modifier = releasing_small_arms
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_small_arms_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

				var:tanks_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = tanks_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_tanks_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = tanks_store_quantity
		var:tanks_store_quantity > 1000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = tanks_store_quantity
				var:tanks_store_quantity > 1000
				var:tanks_store_status = 0
				var:tanks_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = tanks_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

default_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_tanks_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_tanks_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:tanks_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_tanks_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_tanks
				remove_modifier = releasing_tanks
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_tanks_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_tanks_var_1 < 1000000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
		var:tanks_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month_fixe
			value = var:tanks_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_tanks
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_tanks
					multiplier = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_tanks_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_tanks
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_tanks
					multiplier = tanks_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_tanks_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_tanks_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_tanks_1
		# 			multiplier = tanks_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_tanks_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#tanks_release_predicted < stockpiling_tanks_var_state

		tanks_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_tanks_var_state
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_status = 0
		var:tanks_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_tanks = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_var_1
			value = tanks_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_month_fixe
			value = var:tanks_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_release_quantity_1_year
			value = tanks_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_tanks
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_tanks
					multiplier = tanks_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tanks_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tanks_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_quantity
				var:grain_release_quantity > 1000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

default_grain = {

		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_grain_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_grain_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_grain_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_grain
				remove_modifier = releasing_grain
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_grain_var_1 < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_grain
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_grain
					multiplier = grain_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_grain_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_grain
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_grain
					multiplier = grain_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_grain_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_grain_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_grain_1
		# 			multiplier = grain_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state

		grain_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_grain_var_state
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = grain_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity_1_year
			value = grain_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_grain
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_grain
					multiplier = grain_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

		has_variable = fabric_store_quantity
		#var:fabric_store_quantity < 1000000

		var:fabric_release_status = 0
	}

			limit = {
				has_variable = fabric_store_quantity
				#var:fabric_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:fabric_store_status = 0
				var:fabric_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = fabric_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = fabric_store_quantity
		var:fabric_store_quantity > 1000
		var:fabric_store_status = 0
		var:fabric_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = fabric_store_quantity
				var:fabric_store_quantity > 1000
				var:fabric_store_status = 0
				var:fabric_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = fabric_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

		has_variable = fabric_release_quantity
		fabric_release_predicted < stockpiling_fabric_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:fabric_store_status = 0
		var:fabric_release_status = 0

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = fabric_release_quantity
				fabric_release_predicted < stockpiling_fabric_var_state
				var:fabric_store_status = 0
				var:fabric_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = fabric_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_wood
				remove_modifier = releasing_wood
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_wood_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_wood_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_wood_var_1 < 1000000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
		var:wood_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_wood = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_wood_var_1
			value = wood_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month_fixe
			value = var:wood_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_wood
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_wood
					multiplier = wood_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_wood_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_wood_var_1
			value = wood_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_wood
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_wood
					multiplier = wood_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {

set_release_wood_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#wood_release_predicted < stockpiling_wood_var_state

		wood_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_wood_var_state
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
		var:wood_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_wood = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_wood_var_1
			value = wood_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_month_fixe
			value = var:wood_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity_1_year
			value = wood_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_wood
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_wood
					multiplier = wood_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_wood_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#groceries
#quatituy
increase_groceries_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = groceries_store_quantity
		#var:groceries_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:groceries_store_status = 0
		var:groceries_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = groceries_store_quantity
				#var:groceries_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:groceries_store_status = 0
				var:groceries_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = groceries_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_groceries_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = groceries_store_quantity
		var:groceries_store_quantity > 1000
		var:groceries_store_status = 0
		var:groceries_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = groceries_store_quantity
				var:groceries_store_quantity > 1000
				var:groceries_store_status = 0
				var:groceries_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = groceries_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_groceries_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = groceries_release_quantity
		groceries_release_predicted < stockpiling_groceries_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:groceries_store_status = 0
		var:groceries_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = groceries_release_quantity
				groceries_release_predicted < stockpiling_groceries_var_state
				var:groceries_store_status = 0
				var:groceries_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = groceries_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_groceries_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = groceries_release_quantity
		var:groceries_release_quantity > 1000
		var:groceries_store_status = 0
		var:groceries_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = groceries_release_quantity
				var:groceries_release_quantity > 1000
				var:groceries_store_status = 0
				var:groceries_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = groceries_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

			value = clothes_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_clothes
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_clothes
					multiplier = clothes_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_clothes_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_clothes_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_clothes_1
		# 			multiplier = clothes_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_clothes_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#clothes_release_predicted < stockpiling_clothes_var_state

		clothes_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_clothes_var_state
		var:clothes_store_status = 0
		var:clothes_release_status = 0
		var:clothes_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_clothes = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_clothes_var_1
			value = clothes_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_release_month_fixe
			value = var:clothes_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_release_quantity_1_year
			value = clothes_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_clothes
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_clothes
					multiplier = clothes_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = clothes_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_clothes_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#paper
#quatituy
increase_paper_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = paper_store_quantity
		#var:paper_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:paper_store_status = 0
		var:paper_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = paper_store_quantity
				#var:paper_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:paper_store_status = 0
				var:paper_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = paper_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_paper_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = paper_store_quantity
		var:paper_store_quantity > 1000
		var:paper_store_status = 0
		var:paper_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = paper_store_quantity
				var:paper_store_quantity > 1000
				var:paper_store_status = 0
				var:paper_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = paper_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_paper_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = paper_release_quantity
		paper_release_predicted < stockpiling_paper_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:paper_store_status = 0
		var:paper_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = paper_release_quantity
				paper_release_predicted < stockpiling_paper_var_state
				var:paper_store_status = 0
				var:paper_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = paper_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_paper_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = paper_release_quantity
		var:paper_release_quantity > 1000
		var:paper_store_status = 0
		var:paper_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = paper_release_quantity
				var:paper_release_quantity > 1000
				var:paper_store_status = 0
				var:paper_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = paper_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

set_paper_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:paper_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_paper
				remove_modifier = releasing_paper
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_paper_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = paper_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

default_dye = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_dye_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_dye_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:dye_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_dye_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:dye_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_dye
				remove_modifier = releasing_dye
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_dye_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_dye_var_1 < 1000000
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
		var:dye_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_dye = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_dye_var_1
			value = dye_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_dye
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_dye
					multiplier = dye_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_dye_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_dye_var_1
			value = dye_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_dye
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_dye
					multiplier = dye_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}

		# 		}

	}

set_release_dye_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#dye_release_predicted < stockpiling_dye_var_state

		dye_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_dye_var_state
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
		var:dye_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_dye = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_var_1
			value = dye_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity_1_year
			value = dye_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_dye
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_dye
					multiplier = dye_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################
set_coal_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:coal_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_coal
				remove_modifier = releasing_coal
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_coal_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_coal_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_coal_var_1 < 1000000
		var:coal_store_status = 0
		var:coal_release_status = 0
		var:coal_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_coal = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_coal_var_1
			value = coal_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_month_fixe
			value = var:coal_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_coal
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_coal
					multiplier = coal_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_coal_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_coal_var_1
			value = coal_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_coal
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_coal
					multiplier = coal_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_coal_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_coal_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_coal_1
		# 			multiplier = coal_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_coal_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#coal_release_predicted < stockpiling_coal_var_state

		coal_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_coal_var_state
		var:coal_store_status = 0
		var:coal_release_status = 0
		var:coal_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_coal = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_coal_var_1
			value = coal_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_month_fixe
			value = var:coal_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_release_quantity_1_year
			value = coal_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_coal
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_coal
					multiplier = coal_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = coal_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_coal_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_lead_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_lead_var_1 < 1000000
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_lead_var_1
			value = lead_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_lead
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_lead
					multiplier = lead_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_lead_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#lead_release_predicted < stockpiling_lead_var_state

		lead_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_lead_var_state
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = lead_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity_1_year
			value = lead_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_lead
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_lead
					multiplier = lead_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#hardwood
#quatituy
increase_hardwood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = hardwood_store_quantity
		#var:hardwood_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:hardwood_store_status = 0
		var:hardwood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hardwood_store_quantity
				#var:hardwood_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:hardwood_store_status = 0
				var:hardwood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = hardwood_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_hardwood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = hardwood_store_quantity
		var:hardwood_store_quantity > 1000
		var:hardwood_store_status = 0
		var:hardwood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hardwood_store_quantity
				var:hardwood_store_quantity > 1000
				var:hardwood_store_status = 0
				var:hardwood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = hardwood_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_hardwood_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = hardwood_release_quantity
		hardwood_release_predicted < stockpiling_hardwood_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:hardwood_store_status = 0
		var:hardwood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hardwood_release_quantity
				hardwood_release_predicted < stockpiling_hardwood_var_state
				var:hardwood_store_status = 0
				var:hardwood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = hardwood_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_hardwood_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = hardwood_release_quantity
		var:hardwood_release_quantity > 1000
		var:hardwood_store_status = 0
		var:hardwood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hardwood_release_quantity
				var:hardwood_release_quantity > 1000
				var:hardwood_store_status = 0
				var:hardwood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = hardwood_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

		var:hardwood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_hardwood
				remove_modifier = releasing_hardwood
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_hardwood_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = hardwood_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}

					multiplier = rubber_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_rubber_1
		# 			multiplier = rubber_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_rubber_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state

		rubber_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_rubber_var_state
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_rubber = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_var_1
			value = rubber_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_month_fixe
			value = var:rubber_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity_1_year
			value = rubber_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_rubber
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_rubber
					multiplier = rubber_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#oil
#quatituy
increase_oil_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_store_quantity
		#var:oil_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_store_quantity
				#var:oil_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_oil_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_store_quantity
		var:oil_store_quantity > 1000
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_store_quantity
				var:oil_store_quantity > 1000
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_oil_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_release_quantity
		oil_release_predicted < stockpiling_oil_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_release_quantity
				oil_release_predicted < stockpiling_oil_var_state
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_oil_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_release_quantity
		var:oil_release_quantity > 1000
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_release_quantity
				var:oil_release_quantity > 1000
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

set_oil_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_oil
				remove_modifier = releasing_oil
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_oil_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = oil_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

				var:steel_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = steel_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = steel_store_quantity
		var:steel_store_quantity > 1000
		var:steel_store_status = 0
		var:steel_release_status = 0
	}

				var:steel_store_status = 0
				var:steel_release_status = 0

default_steel = {
	is_shown = {
		var:steel_store_status = 0
		var:steel_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_steel_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:steel_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_steel_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:steel_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_steel_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:steel_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_steel
				remove_modifier = releasing_steel
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_steel_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_steel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_steel_var_1 < 1000000
		var:steel_store_status = 0
		var:steel_release_status = 0
		var:steel_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_steel = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_steel_var_1
			value = steel_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_month_fixe
			value = var:steel_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_steel
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_steel
					multiplier = steel_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_steel_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_steel_var_1
			value = steel_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_steel
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_steel
					multiplier = steel_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}

set_release_steel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#steel_release_predicted < stockpiling_steel_var_state

		steel_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_steel_var_state
		var:steel_store_status = 0
		var:steel_release_status = 0
		var:steel_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_steel = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_steel_var_1
			value = steel_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_month_fixe
			value = var:steel_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_release_quantity_1_year
			value = steel_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_steel
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_steel
					multiplier = steel_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = steel_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_steel_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

				name = tools_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_tools_month_store = {

		var:tools_store_month > 12
		var:tools_store_status = 0
		var:tools_release_status = 0
	}
