		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = tools_store_month
				var:tools_store_month > 0
				var:tools_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = tools_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

set_tools_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:tools_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_tools
				remove_modifier = releasing_tools
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tools_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_tools_var_1 < 1000000
		var:tools_store_status = 0
		var:tools_release_status = 0
		var:tools_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_tools = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_tools_var_1
			value = tools_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_month_fixe
			value = var:tools_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_tools
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_tools
					multiplier = tools_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			value = 0

			value = 1000
		}

set_release_tools_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#tools_release_predicted < stockpiling_tools_var_state

		tools_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_tools_var_state
		var:tools_store_status = 0
		var:tools_release_status = 0
		var:tools_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_tools = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tools_var_1
			value = tools_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_month_fixe
			value = var:tools_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_release_quantity_1_year
			value = tools_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_tools
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_tools
					multiplier = tools_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = tools_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_tools_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_automobiles_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_automobiles_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_automobiles_var_1 < 1000000
		var:automobiles_store_status = 0
		var:automobiles_release_status = 0
		var:automobiles_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_automobiles = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_automobiles_var_1
			value = automobiles_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_month_fixe
			value = var:automobiles_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_automobiles
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_automobiles
					multiplier = automobiles_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_automobiles_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_status
			value = 1
		}

		}

			name = automobiles_store_month
			value = 9999

			name = automobiles_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {

set_release_automobiles_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#automobiles_release_predicted < stockpiling_automobiles_var_state

		automobiles_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_automobiles_var_state
		var:automobiles_store_status = 0
		var:automobiles_release_status = 0
		var:automobiles_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_automobiles = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_automobiles_var_1
			value = automobiles_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_month_fixe
			value = var:automobiles_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_release_quantity_1_year
			value = automobiles_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_automobiles
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_automobiles
					multiplier = automobiles_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = automobiles_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_automobiles_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#telephones
#quatituy
increase_telephones_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = telephones_store_quantity
		#var:telephones_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:telephones_store_status = 0
		var:telephones_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = telephones_store_quantity
				#var:telephones_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:telephones_store_status = 0
				var:telephones_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = telephones_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_telephones_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = telephones_store_quantity
		var:telephones_store_quantity > 1000
		var:telephones_store_status = 0
		var:telephones_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = telephones_store_quantity
				var:telephones_store_quantity > 1000
				var:telephones_store_status = 0
				var:telephones_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = telephones_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_telephones_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = telephones_release_quantity
		telephones_release_predicted < stockpiling_telephones_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:telephones_store_status = 0
		var:telephones_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = telephones_release_quantity
				telephones_release_predicted < stockpiling_telephones_var_state
				var:telephones_store_status = 0
				var:telephones_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = telephones_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_telephones_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = telephones_release_quantity
		var:telephones_release_quantity > 1000
		var:telephones_store_status = 0
		var:telephones_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = telephones_release_quantity
				var:telephones_release_quantity > 1000
				var:telephones_store_status = 0
				var:telephones_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = telephones_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_variable = {
			name = radios_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_radios
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_radios
					multiplier = radios_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
		# validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes
		# every_scope_building = {
		# 	if  = {
		# 		limit = {
		# 			is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		}
		# 		remove_modifier = release_radios_1
		# 		remove_modifier = store_radios_1
		# 		add_modifier = {
		# 			name = store_radios_1
		# 			multiplier = radios_store_for_modifier
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# }
	}
}
set_release_radios_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#radios_release_predicted < stockpiling_radios_var_state

		radios_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_radios_var_state
		var:radios_store_status = 0
		var:radios_release_status = 0
		var:radios_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_radios = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_radios_var_1
			value = radios_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_release_month_fixe
			value = var:radios_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_release_quantity_1_year
			value = radios_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_radios
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_radios
					multiplier = radios_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = radios_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_radios_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#opium
#quatituy
increase_opium_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = opium_store_quantity
		#var:opium_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:opium_store_status = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opium_store_quantity
				#var:opium_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:opium_store_status = 0
				var:opium_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = opium_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_opium_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = opium_store_quantity
		var:opium_store_quantity > 1000
		var:opium_store_status = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opium_store_quantity
				var:opium_store_quantity > 1000
				var:opium_store_status = 0
				var:opium_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = opium_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_opium_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = opium_release_quantity
		opium_release_predicted < stockpiling_opium_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:opium_store_status = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opium_release_quantity
				opium_release_predicted < stockpiling_opium_var_state
				var:opium_store_status = 0
				var:opium_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = opium_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_opium_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = opium_release_quantity
		var:opium_release_quantity > 1000
		var:opium_store_status = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opium_release_quantity
				var:opium_release_quantity > 1000
				var:opium_store_status = 0
				var:opium_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = opium_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

				add = 12
			}
		}
	}

		has_variable = opium_store_month

		var:opium_release_status = 0

				var:opium_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = opium_store_month

			}
		}
	}
}

set_opium_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:opium_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_opium
				remove_modifier = releasing_opium
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_opium_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_month
			value = 12
		}
	}
}
set_store_opium_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_opium_var_1 < 1000000
		var:opium_store_status = 0
		var:opium_release_status = 0
		var:opium_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_opium = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_opium_var_1
			value = opium_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_month_fixe
			value = var:opium_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = storing_opium
				add_modifier = {
					name = storing_opium
					multiplier = opium_store_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

set_release_opium = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_opium_var_1
			value = opium_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_month_fixe
			value = var:opium_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_release_quantity_1_year
			value = opium_release_predicted
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				remove_modifier = releasing_opium
				add_modifier = {
					name = releasing_opium
					multiplier = opium_release_quantity_1_week
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = opium_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_opium_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#ammunition

	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_ammunition_var
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
ammunition_sell_off = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_ammunition_var
			value = 0
		}

	}
}

		var:trade_ammunition_var = 1
	}

update_stocked_goods_global_variable_list = { 
	effect = {
		clear_global_variable_list = stocked_goods_global_variable_list

 		#ammunition
		if = {
			limit = {
				stockpiling_ammunition_var_state > 0
			}
			add_to_global_variable_list = {
				name = stocked_goods_global_variable_list
				target = global_var:stocked_ammunition_flag_global_variable
			}
		} 
 		#small_arms
		if = {
			limit = {
				stockpiling_small_arms_var_state > 0
			}
			add_to_global_variable_list = {
				name = stocked_goods_global_variable_list
				target = global_var:stocked_small_arms_flag_global_variable
			}
		} 
 		#artillery
		if = {
			limit = {
				stockpiling_artillery_var_state > 0
			}
			add_to_global_variable_list = {
				name = stocked_goods_global_variable_list
				target = global_var:stocked_artillery_flag_global_variable
			}
		} 
 		#tanks
		if = {
			limit = {
				stockpiling_tanks_var_state > 0
			}
			add_to_global_variable_list = {
				name = stocked_goods_global_variable_list
				target = global_var:stocked_tanks_flag_global_variable
			}
		} 
 		#aeroplanes
		if = {
			limit = {
				stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state > 0
			}
			add_to_global_variable_list = {

			}
		}

REPLACE:set_store_ammunition_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_ammunition_var_1 < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		var:ammunition_store_quantity > 0 
		has_technology_researched = percussion_cap
	}
} 
REPLACE:set_store_tanks_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_tanks_var_1 < 1000000
		var:tanks_store_status = 0
